**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go**, which creates three main tables:\\n\\n1. **alert table** - Stores dashboard-level alerts with fields like dashboard_id, panel_id, name, message, state, settings, frequency, handler, severity, silenced, execution_error, eval_data, eval_date, new_state_date, state_changes, created, updated\\n2. **alert_notification table** - Stores notification channels/handlers with org_id, name, type, settings, is_default, frequency, send_reminder, disable_resolve_message, uid, secure_settings\\n3. **alert_notification_state table** - Tracks notification delivery state with org_id, alert_id, notifier_id, state, version, updated_at, alert_rule_state_updated_version\\n4. **alert_rule_tag table** - Tags for legacy alerts (alert_id and tag_id)\\n\\n## Unified Alerting (ngalert) System\\n\\nThe unified alerting system is implemented in **pkg/services/ngalert/** with the following key components:\\n\\n### Core Service\\n- **ngalert.go** - Main AlertNG service that initializes all alerting components, sets up HTTP routes, and integrates with other Grafana services\\n- **models/alert_rule.go** - Defines AlertRule struct and NoDataState/ExecutionErrorState enums\\n\\n### Alert Rule Storage\\n- **store/alert_rule.go** - Implements DBstore for persisting alert rules with functions like DeleteAlertRulesByUID, CreateAlertRule, UpdateAlertRule\\n- **store/alertmanager.go** - Handles Alertmanager configuration storage\\n- **store/compat.go** - Database conversion functions: alertRuleToModelsAlertRule() and alertRuleFromModelsAlertRule()\\n\\n### Scheduling and Evaluation\\n- **schedule/alert_rule.go** - AlertRuleEvaluator that evaluates individual alert rules\\n- **schedule/schedule.go** - AlertsSched that schedules alert rule evaluation across all organizations\\n- **eval/eval.go** - ConditionEvaluator that evaluates alert conditions and executes pipelines\\n\\n### State Management\\n- **state/manager.go** - Manager that tracks alert instance states with Firing, Normal, Pending, NoData, Error states\\n- **state/state.go** - Alert state definitions and transitions\\n- **state/compat.go** - Compatibility functions like IsKeepLastStateCompatible() for legacy state conversion\\n- **state/historian/** - Tracks alert state history for audit and debugging\\n\\n### Notification Handling\\n- **notifier/alertmanager.go** - Integration with Prometheus Alertmanager\\n- **notifier/legacy_storage/** - Compatibility layer for legacy alert notifications:\\n  - **config.go** - DeserializeAlertmanagerConfig() and SerializeAlertmanagerConfig() for Alertmanager configuration\\n  - **compat.go** - Converts legacy notification channels to Prometheus receiver format\\n  - **persist.go** - Persistence interface for alertmanager configuration\\n  - **receivers.go** - Legacy receiver handling\\n\\n### Provisioning\\n- **provisioning/alert_rules.go** - Handles
